In patients with pure Lewy body Parkinson's disease, previous post-mortem studies have shown that dopaminergic</span></span></div></div></div><div class="jss537"><div class="jss538"><div class="MuiTypography-root jss539 jss540 MuiTypography-body1" data-testid="peer-paper-title" id="peer-paper-title"><a href="/CZ/en/tech-docs/paper/567824"><span>Evidence-based morphine dosing for postoperative neonates and infants.</span></a></div><div class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-caption">Elke H J Krekels et al.</div><div class="MuiTypography-root jss544 jss545 MuiTypography-body1"><span>Clinical pharmacokinetics, 53(6), 553-563 (2014-02-06)</span></div><div class=""><span class="MuiTypography-root jss543 MuiTypography-body2"><span>From a previously validated paediatric population pharmacokinetic model, it was derived that non-linear morphine maintenance doses of 5 μg/kg(1.5)/h, with a 50 % dose reduction in neonates with a postnatal age (PNA) &lt;10 days, yield similar morphine and metabolite concentrations</span></span></div></div></div><div class="MuiTypography-root jss536 MuiTypography-body1"><a href="/CZ/en/search/34851?focus=papers&amp;page=1&amp;perpage=30&amp;sort=relevance&amp;term=34851&amp;type=citation_search" role="link" tabindex="0">View All Related Papers</a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="pdpGrid__section"><div data-testid="pdp-protocols-articles"><div class="MuiContainer-root MuiContainer-maxWidthLg"><button class="jss185" disabled="" type="button"><h2 class="MuiTypography-root MuiTypography-h2">Protocols and Articles</h2></button></div><div class="MuiCollapse-root" style="min-height: 0px;
